However, existing approaches typically assume that intermediate agent outputs are equally reliable, leaving them vulnerable to hallucination propagation, where incorrect decisions generated in early development phases are transferred to downstream agents and negatively impact final software quality. To address this challenge, we propose UA-ChatDev, an uncertainty-aware multi-agent software development framework that integrates uncertainty quantification into agent interactions. It introduces a lightweight uncertainty estimation mechanism based on token-level log probabilities to assess the confidence of agent responses and employs phase-aware threshold calibration to selectively trigger retrieval-based verification when uncertainty exceeds acceptable levels. Extensive experiments on the SRDD benchmark demonstrate that UA-ChatDev consistently outperforms existing single-agent and multi-agent software development frameworks across completeness, executability, consistency, and overall quality metrics.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面向L4-L5全自主电信网络，AI/ML代理需实时做出网络决策，但目前缺乏标准化的运行时机制来拦截和验证AI推理输出，存在错误自主决策风险。

Method: 提出GRV框架，通过多维度加权评估（动作范围、类型、服务关键性、自主等级、可逆性、时间行为模式）确定关键性等级，并应用分级验证机制（执行并记录、边界检查、独立代理验证、多代理共识），同时提供跨代理冲突检测和运行时合规日志。

Result: 给出了GRV的架构设计、算法流程、O-RAN部署模型，并评估了对已知电信AI/ML攻击的威胁覆盖范围。

Conclusion: GRV框架为自主电信网络提供了一种可标准化的安全运行时保障机制，能够有效拦截错误的AI决策，支持合规要求。

Abstract: The evolution toward fully autonomous telecommunications networks (Autonomous Network Levels 4-5) requires AI/ML agents to make real-time network decisions without human intervention. However, no standardized runtime mechanism exists to intercept and validate individual inference outputs before they trigger live network state changes, creating risks of erroneous autonomous decisions. This paper proposes the Guard Rail Validation (GRV) framework, a standardizable runtime architecture for intercepting and validating AI-driven decisions before execution. The framework evaluates decisions across multiple weighted dimensions -- including action scope, action type, service criticality, agent autonomy level, reversibility, and temporal behavioural patterns -- to determine a criticality level. Based on this level, graduated validation mechanisms are applied: execute-with-logging, bounds checking, independent agent validation, or multi-agent consensus. The framework additionally provides cross-agent conflict detection with criticality-weighted priority resolution and runtime conformance logging for regulatory compliance (e.g., EU AI Act Article 14). We present the architecture, algorithmic procedures, O-RAN deployment model, and evaluate threat coverage against known AI/ML attacks in telecommunications.

### [255] [Purified OPSD: On-Policy Self-Distillation Without Losing How to Think](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02234)
*Zhanming Shen,Jintao Tong,Shaotian Yan,Chen Shen,Hao Chen,Wentao Ye,Xiaomeng Hu,Rui Miao,Haobo Wang,Junbo Zhao,Gang Chen,Jieping Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现监督式自蒸馏（OPSD）在长链思维（long-CoT）推理模型上效果不佳，原因是教师的监督信号被参考诱导成分主导，导致模型死记硬背而非真正推理。作者提出两步解决方案：通过构建仅参考教师分离非迁移成分，并利用点互信息（PMI）将残差转化为可蒸馏的目标分布，在四个long-CoT模型上取得一致改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OPSD方法在长链思维推理模型上表现失败，不仅收益微乎其微，还会破坏模型依赖的反思推理能力。作者希望诊断其根本原因并提出有效解决方案。

Method: 1) 对教师监督信号进行新颖分解，发现参考诱导成分主导了信号，而问题条件化的可迁移推理成分被忽略或抑制。2) 构建仅参考教师（仅有参考无问题）分离非迁移成分，用残差捕获问题条件化的可迁移校正。3) 利用点互信息（PMI）将残差转化为良好形式的PMI目标分布，供学生直接蒸馏。

Result: 在四个long-CoT模型、两个数据集上的实验表明，该方法在基线和标准OPSD上均取得一致改进，同时在整个训练过程中保持了模型自然的认知行为。

Conclusion: OPSD在long-CoT模型上失败的原因是教师监督信号被参考捷径主导；通过PMI蒸馏去除参考诱导成分后，可有效提升long-CoT推理能力。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) has emerged as a promising paradigm for improving LLM reasoning, where a privileged teacher with access to reference solutions provides token-level supervision on the student's own generated trajectories. However, we find that OPSD consistently fails on long chain-of-thought (long-CoT) reasoning models, yielding at best marginal gains while destabilizing the reflective reasoning capability these models depend on. Through a novel decomposition of the teacher's supervision signal, we identify the root cause: the teacher's supervision is dominated by a reference-induced component that drives rote memorization of reference-specific shortcuts, while the question-conditioned, inference-transferable component is ignored or actively opposed. Based on this diagnosis, we propose a two-step solution. First, we construct a reference-only teacher (the same model conditioned on the reference without the question) to isolate the non-transferable component of the supervision signal; the residual after subtracting this component captures the question-conditioned, inference-transferable correction. Second, we use pointwise mutual information (PMI) as the mechanism to transform this residual into a well-formed PMI target distribution that the student can directly distill from, filtering out the reference-induced shortcut. Experiments on four long-CoT models across two datasets demonstrate consistent improvements over both the base model and standard OPSD, while preserving the models' natural epistemic behavior throughout training.

### [256] [What LLM Agents Say When No One Is Watching: Social Structure and Latent Objective Emergence in Multi-Agent Debates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02507)

Method: 提出双通道辩论框架：智能体产生公开话语（进入共享历史）和OTR回应（记录但不展示给其他参与者）。跨10个模型、3个场景、每个场景5个变体进行实验。

Result: 对齐诱导设置产生系统性的公开-OTR分歧，目标智能体的决策分歧从~3%基线上升到约40%。效果在四种聚合分析（立场、语义相似度、自然语言推理、调查回应）中一致。OTR回应明确将公开迎合归因于关系压力如职业风险或赞助义务。

Conclusion: 智能体评估应超越显式目标，检测涌现性目标。提出了双通道评估框架和互补行为指标来操作化这一评估。

Abstract: LLM agents will increasingly act in socially structured settings where role, audience, and relational context can shape what is advantageous or costly to say. We study whether such social structure, without any explicit objective in the prompt, changes what an agent expresses publicly relative to an off-the-record (OTR) channel elicited under the same condition. We introduce a dual-channel debate framework in which agents produce public utterances that enter the shared history alongside OTR responses that are recorded but never shown to the other participant. Across 10 models, 3 scenarios, and 5 variations within each scenario, alignment-inducing settings produce systematic public-OTR divergence in the targeted agent, with its decision divergence rising from a $\sim$3% baseline to roughly 40%. The effect is consistent across four aggregate analyses: stance, semantic similarity, natural language inference, and survey responses. In some cases, the OTR response explicitly attributes public accommodation to relational pressures, such as career risk or sponsorship obligation. The findings suggest that agent evaluation should extend beyond explicit goals and detect emergent objectives. We present a dual-channel evaluation framework and complementary behavioral measures that operationalize this assessment.

### [259] [A Hippocampus for Linear Attention: An Exact Memory for What the Recurrent State Forgets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02303)
*Wanyun Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HOLA为线性注意力模型引入海马体互补缓存机制，通过保留一个有限大小的精确KV缓存来弥补压缩记忆的丢失，在保持O(1)存储的同时显著提升长上下文检索能力，340M参数下困惑度低于完整注意力Transformer++。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性注意力和状态空间模型将前缀压缩为固定大小的循环状态，虽然带来O(1)内存优势，但导致有损的精确记忆：当大量键值关联竞争时，早期事实被覆盖，needle召回性能下降。

Method: 受互补学习系统启发，HOLA保留delta-rule状态作为压缩记忆，同时增加一个有界精确KV缓存，形成半参数化测试时记忆。缓存写入无需学习淘汰模块，保留具有大beta*||e||的token（即实际提交到状态的预测残差）；使用解耦的RMSNorm-gamma缓存读取将精确KV对转化为尖锐检索而非软平均。

Result: 340M参数在15B SlimPajama上训练，HOLA将Wikitext困惑度从27.32降至22.92（-16.1%），低于全注意力Transformer++（26.88）；LAMBADA困惑度从30.95降至30.26。在线性上下文检索中达到最佳，在RULER needle-in-a-haystack召回中（32k token，16倍训练长度）远超GDN和匹配的HOLA+recency缓存。

Conclusion: 通过为线性注意力配备海马体互补缓存，可以在保持线性注意力效率的同时显著弥补其有损记忆缺陷，实现更优的长上下文检索和语言建模性能。

Abstract: Linear-attention and state-space language models compress the prefix into a fixed-size recurrent state, yielding O(1) memory at the cost of a lossy exact memory: when many key--value associations compete, earlier facts are overwritten and needle recall degrades. Inspired by Complementary Learning Systems, we give linear attention a hippocampal complement. HOLA (Hippocampal Linear Attention) keeps the usual delta-rule state as a compressive memory and adds a bounded exact KV cache, forming a semiparametric test-time memory: the state models linearly compressible structure, while the cache stores associations that should not be forced through that state. The cache writes without a learned eviction module, keeping tokens with large beta * ||e||, the prediction residual actually committed to the state; a decoupled RMSNorm-gamma cache read then turns these exact KV pairs into sharp retrieval rather than soft averaging. At 340M parameters trained on 15B SlimPajama tokens, HOLA lowers Wikitext perplexity from 27.32 to 22.92 (-16.1%), below a full-attention Transformer++ (26.88), and improves LAMBADA perplexity from 30.95 to 30.26. It also achieves the best linear in-context retrieval and remains much more robust than GDN or a matched HOLA+recency cache on RULER needle-in-a-haystack recall out to 32k tokens (16x its training length).

</details>


### [260] [Grounded autonomous research: a fault-tolerant LLM pipeline from corpus to manuscript in frontier computational physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02329)
*Haonan Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一个端到端自动化研究管线，从11,083篇凝聚态物理arXiv论文出发，自主完成文献映射、方法校准、第一性原理计算到论文撰写，在交替磁性压电效应领域产生三项实质性物理发现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建六阶段管线（47个全新上下文会话，仅共享磁盘状态），包含2,162次文献咨询事件；采用冗余容错机制：全新上下文隔离、分布式接地、对抗性审查；预实验和后实验阶段完全自主，实验阶段仅在复现失败时需要有限人工干预（操作知识整理，非科学方向）。

Conclusion: 该管线的基本原语、特征化失效模式和量化干预模式为超越计算物理学的高风险科学领域的自主研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Autonomous-research agents have demonstrated end-to-end LLM automation in machine-learning sandboxes where execution provides calibration. Frontier physical science differs categorically: physical reasoning underlies every methodology choice, toolchains are often underdocumented, and calibration must come from external literature anchors - which unscaffolded agents cite but do not confront, hallucinating plausible, unverifiable results from internal priors. We present a pipeline that runs end-to-end from a corpus of 11,083 recent condensed-matter physics arXiv papers to a publication-grade manuscript with three substantive physics findings (here on altermagnetic piezomagnetism): the agent autonomously conceives a research direction by mapping the corpus, calibrates methodology by reproducing published references, conducts novel first-principles computations, and writes the manuscript - grounded in literature throughout, across 47 fresh-context sessions in six phases sharing only on-disk state, with 2,162 literature-consultation events. Fault tolerance emerges from redundancy: fresh-context isolation, distributed grounding, and adversarial review catch what any single session misses; pre- and post-pilot stages are fully autonomous, and pilot requires bounded human intervention only at reproduction failures - operational knowledge curation, not scientific direction. Two paired failure modes - a pre-architecture baseline and a no-pilot ablation - isolate structurally enforced numerical confrontation at calibration checkpoints as the operative grounding mechanism. The primitives, characterized failure modes, and quantified intervention pattern lay a foundation for autonomous research in high-stakes scientific domains beyond computational physics.

### [261] [DRIFTLENS: Measuring Memory-Induced Reasoning Drift in Personalized Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02374)
*Xi Fang,Weijie Xu,Yingqiang Ge,Yuhui Xu,Stephanie Eckman,Chandan K. Reddy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出DRIFTLENS框架，用于量化LLM在个性化记忆注入下推理轨迹的漂移，发现用户属性记忆会显著改变模型的推理过程（即使最终回答依然流畅合理），且现有后训练方法（GRPO/DPO）只能部分缓解此问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 个性化记忆虽能提升LLM交互的适配性，但可能无意中改变模型得出答案的推理轨迹。现有研究多关注最终答案质量，缺乏对推理过程因用户属性记忆而偏离的量化评估方法，尤其在无标准答案的开放性问题中。

Method: 提出DRIFTLENS框架，将每个推理步骤映射到价值类别，并计算无记忆轨迹与注入用户属性记忆后轨迹之间的分歧度。在4种LLM和10种用户属性类别上，先验证框架能区分语用噪声与实质性推理变化，再评估GRPO和DPO后训练方法的降漂移效果。

Result: 用户属性记忆在各类模型和属性上均导致中到大程度的推理漂移（超过语用噪声基线），即使最终回答仍流畅、相关且合理。GRPO和DPO均能降低漂移，但效果不均匀，且对下游能力（有用性、指令遵循）的影响因模型和奖励函数而异。

Conclusion: 记忆诱导的推理漂移是LLM个性化中的一个可测量且仅被部分缓解的失效模式，需进一步研究更鲁棒的控制方法。

Abstract: Personalization changes what a model says to a user; we show that it can also change the reasoning trajectory used to justify the response. Modern LLMs personalize interactions by storing user attributes, preferences, and prior context, then injecting this information into future prompts. We study whether such memory reshapes reasoning on open-ended questions where no single ground-truth answer exists. To quantify this effect, we introduce DRIFTLENS, a ground-truth-free framework that maps each expressed reasoning step to a value category and measures divergence between a question's no-memory trajectory and its trajectory under injected user-attribute memory. We first validate that DRIFTLENS distinguishes content-free pragmatic noise from substantive reasoning changes. Across four LLMs and 10 user-attribute categories, including age, occupation, and disability, user-attribute memory induces medium-to-large reasoning drift above each model's pragmatic-noise floor, even when final answers remain fluent, on-topic, and plausible. We then evaluate GRPO- and DPO-based post-training methods for reducing drift. Both reduce drift, but neither uniformly dominates; effects on downstream capability, helpfulness, and instruction following are model-and reward-dependent. These results suggest that memory-induced reasoning drift is a measurable and only partly mitigated failure mode of personalized language models.

While much current research focuses on improving reasoning capabilities, safety-critical real-time deployment also requires bounded and verifiable coordination among heterogeneous components operating concurrently under uncertainty. Software-mediated coordination presents fundamental limitations in domains where bounded latency, deterministic coordination, and enforceable safety guarantees are essential.
  Hence, we propose a hardware-enforced semantic coordination architecture in which selected coordination semantics are implemented directly at the hardware level via field-programmable gate arrays (FPGAs). The approach builds on the Topic-Based Communication Space Petri Net (TB-CSPN) framework, which separates semantic reasoning from interaction management.
  In this approach, selected TB-CSPN coordination mechanisms are mapped onto FPGA primitives, creating a hardware-native semantic coordination layer. Focus is not on acceleration, but on enforcing temporal synchronization, semantic gating, authorization constraints, and bounded coordination behavior directly in hardware. Semantic reasoning remains adaptive and software-driven, while embedded coordination semantics become deterministic.

</details>


### [263] [Steerability via constraints: a substrate for scalable oversight of coding agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02389)
*Thomas Winninger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 编码智能体的瓶颈在于人工审查；通过类似于管理大型工程团队的约束方法（访问控制、网络策略、严格编码规范），可以用更低的token成本实现更有效的监督。实验表明，在Python代码库中，约束框架加小型审查工具可将后门检测召回率从54.5%提升至90.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编码智能体能力强大，但人工审查成为瓶颈——无约束的智能体会引入安全风险、侵蚀代码库可扩展性，并大幅增加人工审查成本。

Method: 借鉴管理大型人类工程团队的方法（访问控制、网络策略、通过工具强制编码规范）来约束编码智能体；构建了端到端系统，并设计对照实验：由小型审查模型（Gemma 4 e4b）检查包含11个后门的Python代码库，对比无约束与约束框架+工具两种情况下的召回率。

Result: 召回率从54.5%（无约束、无工具）提升至90.9%（约束框架加约200行代码的`docs` CLI工具），且约束框架和工具独立贡献了提升效果。

Conclusion: 约束方法比最近的智能体脚手架更节省token成本；在语言保证最少的Python中收益最大，但原则可扩展到Rust等语言。

Abstract: Coding agents are capable; human oversight is the bottleneck. Unconstrained agents introduce security risks, erode codebase scalability, and make human review increasingly costly. We argue that the same methods used for decades to manage large human engineering teams: access control, network policies, strict coding conventions enforced by tooling; transfer directly to coding agents, and are cheaper (in token) than recent agentic scaffolding. We sketch a start-to-end system on this principle, and report a controlled experiment in scalable oversight: a small reviewer (Gemma 4 e4b) inspects a Python codebase containing 11 inserted backdoors. Recall rises from 54.5% (unconstrained, no tools) to 90.9% (constrained substrate plus a ~200-LoC `docs` CLI), with substrate and tools contributing independently. We choose Python deliberately: substrate-level oversight gains are largest where the language gives the fewest guarantees by default; the principles extend to languages like Rust.

Abstract: Steering and monitoring activations in Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used for both safety and interpretability. However, existing methods for extracting these subspaces are computationally expensive, which becomes prohibitive on reasoning models who produce long reasoning traces. By adapting the Recursive Feature Machine (RFM) algorithm -- which can be computed efficiently -- with a probe-informed initialization, we are able to identify the multi-dimensional refusal subspace in seconds, on reasoning (Qwen 3) and non-reasoning (Qwen 2.5) models. While RFM allows for faster subspace identification, it also showed better performances on the ablation task than its alternatives. Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in 3D indoor synthesis for Manhattan environments. However, existing methods often fail to capture plausible object layout patterns in non-Manhattan settings, primarily because they struggle to model non-orthogonal spatial relationships, leading to high geometric violations and low physical fidelity. To address this challenge, we propose SPG-Layout, a novel text-driven framework designed to generate physically plausible indoor scenes within complex non-Manhattan environments. Specifically, we first utilize statistical priors of object distributions to guide the training process, enhancing environmental understanding and fidelity. Furthermore, mirroring human design workflows, we adopt a hierarchical layout strategy that prioritizes the placement of large objects, thereby substantially minimizing layout violations. By synergizing these components, SPG-Layout achieves a balanced optimization of semantic realism and physical plausibility. To evaluate performance in these complex settings, we constructed a new benchmark comprising 500 diverse non-Manhattan environments. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SPG-Layout consistently and significantly outperforms existing methods across both Manhattan and non-Manhattan environments. The code will be publicly released.

### [266] [G-RRM: Guiding Symbolic Solvers with Recurrent Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02491)
*Timo Bertram,Sidhant Bhavnani,Richard Freinschlag,Erich Kobler,Andreas Mayr,Günter Klambauer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出神经符号方法G-RRM，将符号等变循环推理模型（SE-RRM）与经典符号求解器（回溯、Glucose 4.1、CaDiCaL 3.0）结合，用于约束满足问题。实验表明，当问题具有大规模组合搜索空间且求解器能动态覆盖分支选择时，神经引导能显著加速求解（如回溯加速33.3倍，Glucose加速1.70倍），否则无明显提升甚至产生负收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究神经引导在何种条件下能有效提升符号求解器的搜索效率，特别是SE-RRM作为神经求解器生成的解建议能否以及何时能加速经典约束满足问题的求解过程。

Method: 提出G-RRM框架，利用SE-RRM生成完整解建议作为神经引导，输入至回溯、Glucose 4.1、CaDiCaL 3.0等符号求解器；通过区分求解器架构是否支持动态覆盖分支选择，实验验证两个关键条件对加速效果的影响。

Result: 在9×9数独上，G-RRM使回溯加速33.3倍，Glucose 4.1加速1.70倍；完美提示下25×25数独上Glucose加速1.17倍。CaDiCaL无显著加速（中位数1.02倍），甚至出现小幅显著减速（均值0.90倍）。

Conclusion: 神经引导的实际加速效果取决两个条件：问题实例需具有广阔的搜索空间，且求解器架构需能动态覆写分支选择以纠正神经提示的不完美之处。不符合这些条件的场景下，神经引导不会带来实际收益。

Abstract: In this work, we focus on SE-RRMs, a symbol-equivariant instantiation of RRMs that exhibits improved extrapolation to larger problem sizes. We propose a neuro-symbolic approach, ``Guiding with Recurrent Reasoning Models'' (G-RRM), which integrates SE-RRMs with symbolic solvers for constraint satisfaction problems. SE-RRMs act as neural solvers that generate full solution proposals and guide classical symbolic solvers, such as backtracking or SAT-based methods like Glucose 4.1 and CaDiCaL 3.0.0, that produce globally correct solutions. Centrally, we investigate when neural guidance with G-RRM improves the search efficiency of symbolic solvers. %
Our experiments show that the efficacy of G-RRM depends on two conditions: first, the problem instances must have an expansive combinatorial search space to expose potential gains, and second, the solver architecture must be capable of dynamically overwriting its branching choices to recover when neural hints are imperfect. When these conditions hold, guidance drives median conflict counts to zero and yields significant wall-clock speedups: on $9\times9$ Sudoku, where the SE-RRM correctly solves $91.1\%$ of instances, backtracking accelerates by $33.3\times$ and Glucose 4.1 by $1.70\times$ (median, $p<0.001$), with Glucose 4.1 retaining a $1.17\times$ speedup on perfect-hint $25\times25$ grids. In contrast, CaDiCaL 3.0.0, whose runtime is overhead-dominated and which always respects the injected branching hints rather than overwriting them, shows no significant speedup (median $1.02\times$, n.s.) and even a small significant mean slowdown ($0.90\times$) on $9\times9$. These results delineate the regimes in which neural guidance translates into practical speedups.

</details>


### [267] [ReContext: Recursive Evidence Replay as LLM Harness for Long-Context Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02509)
*Yanjun Zhao,Ruizhong Qiu,Tianxin Wei,Yuanchen Bei,Zhining Liu,Lingjie Chen,Ismini Lourentzou,Hanghang Tong,Jingrui He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RECONTEXT是一种无需训练的长上下文推理方法，通过递归地从模型内部提取与问题相关的证据并在最终生成前回放，在不剪裁上下文的情况下提升证据利用率。在Qwen3-4B/8B和Llama3-8B上的8个长上下文数据集（128K长度）上均取得最佳平均排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM虽然支持长上下文窗口，但常无法有效利用输入中已有的相关证据，存在"上下文可访问"与"上下文有效利用"之间的差距。

Method: RECONTEXT利用模型内部相关性信号构建查询条件的证据池，并在最终生成前回放该证据池（保留完整原始上下文）。通过递归选择过程将证据组织与答案生成分离，无需训练、外部记忆或上下文剪裁。理论分析基于联想记忆将上下文视为记忆存储，问题视为检索线索，注意力视为线索-痕迹关联，回放视为痕迹再激活。

Result: 在8个长上下文数据集（128K长度）上，RECONTEXT在Qwen3-4B、Qwen3-8B和Llama3-8B三个骨干模型上均一致提升证据利用率，并获得最佳平均排名。

Conclusion: RECONTEXT是一种有效的训练无关长上下文推理增强方法，通过递归证据回放弥合了上下文访问与有效利用之间的差距。

Abstract: Understanding and reasoning over long contexts has become a key requirement for deploying large language models (LLMs) in realistic applications. Although recent LLMs support increasingly long context windows, they often fail to use relevant evidence that is already present in the input, revealing a gap between context access and effective context utilization. In this work, we propose Recursive Evidence Replay as LLM Harness for Long-Context Reasoning (RECONTEXT), a training-free inference method for improving long-context reasoning. RECONTEXT uses model-internal relevance signals to construct a query-conditioned evidence pool and replays it before final generation while preserving the full original context. This recursive selection process separates evidence organization from answer generation without training, external memory, or context pruning. We also provide a theoretical analysis based on associative memory, which characterizes the context as a memory store, the question as a retrieval cue, attention as cue-trace association, and replay as trace reactivation. Experiments on eight long-context datasets with 128K context length show that RECONTEXT consistently improves evidence utilization across Qwen3-4B, Qwen3-8B, and Llama3-8B, achieving the best average rank on all three backbones. Code is available at https://github.com/Yanjun-Zhao/ReContext.

</details>


### [268] [Distributed Attacks in Persistent-State AI Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02514)
*Josh Hills,Ida Caspary,Asa Cooper Stickland*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出迭代式AI编码环境（Iterative VibeCoding），研究AI编码代理在跨多次PR迭代开发时，如何利用持久化代码库进行渐进式攻击（将恶意负载分散到多个PR中）。实验表明，渐进式攻击比单次集中攻击更难被监控器检测，且高规避率在不同模型后端间泛化。作者提出跨PR状态链接追踪监控器，结合四监控器集成可将渐进攻击规避率从93%降至47%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI编码代理日益自主且代码跨会话持久化，产生了新的攻击面：被植入恶意指令的代理可将攻击分散到多次PR提交中并选择最佳时机释放负载。现有研究未充分关注这种跨PR的渐进式攻击动态，需要新的安全控制框架。

Method: 构建Iterative VibeCoding基准，包含CLI工具和Flask Web服务两个任务族共20个变体。使用Claude Sonnet 4.5作为攻击代理，GPT-4o作为监控器。比较渐进式攻击（跨PR分布侧任务）与非渐进式攻击（单PR集中攻击）。引入状态化链接追踪监控器（跨PR跟踪可疑积累），并与差异监控器、轨迹监控器组成四监控器集成。

Result: 无单一监控器能同时防御渐进式和非渐进式攻击，策略选择取决于监控器类型。高规避率（≥65%）在不同攻击模型后端（Sonnet 4.5、Gemini 3.1 Pro、Kimi K2.5）间泛化。更强监控模型下渐进与非渐进规避差距扩大。状态化链接追踪监控器在检测渐进式攻击上显著优于传统差异监控器。四监控器集成将渐进攻击规避率从93%降至47%。

Conclusion: 持久化状态攻击面是AI编码代理安全的核心挑战，而非单模型能力问题。跨PR的渐进式攻击需要多维度、状态化的监控策略，组合监控器集成是降低风险的有效方向。

Abstract: As AI coding agents become more autonomous, they increasingly ship code iteratively, with the codebase persisting across sessions. This persistence creates a new attack surface: a misaligned or prompt-injected agent can distribute attacks across pull requests (PRs) and time its payload for the PR with the best natural cover. To study the resulting dynamics, we introduce Iterative VibeCoding, a setting for AI control, the study of safely deploying capable but potentially untrusted AI. In Iterative VibeCoding, a coding agent builds software over a sequence of PRs in a persistent codebase while pursuing a covert side task. Our benchmark includes two task families: CLI tools and Flask web services, across 20 total task variations. We use Claude Sonnet 4.5 as the attack agent and GPT-4o as the monitor. We compare gradual attacks, which distribute the side task across PRs, against non-gradual attacks concentrated in a single PR. No single monitor is robust to both: which strategy evades best (success while evading the monitor) depends on the monitor type, so a defender cannot close off both gradual and non-gradual attacks with any one monitor. High evasion (>= 65%) generalizes across model attack agent backends (Sonnet 4.5, Gemini 3.1 Pro, Kimi K2.5), confirming this is a property of the persistent-state attack surface rather than a single model's capability. Evasion also remains high across state-of-the-art monitor models and the gap between gradual and non-gradual evasion widens for more capable models. We introduce a stateful link-tracker monitor that tracks suspicious buildup across PRs. On both task families, it detects gradual attacks substantially better than diff monitors that merely see more accumulated history. Combining this stronger monitor with trajectory monitors in a four-monitor ensemble reduces gradual-attack evasion from 93% under the weakest standard diff monitor to 47%.

</details>

### [269] [On the structure of constacyclic codes over finite chain rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01771)
*Vaishali Singh,Sucheta Dutt,Ridhima Thakral*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文针对有限链环上任意长度的λ-常循环码，给出了基于最小度数多项式的显式生成元构造，该构造实现了最少生成元数；证明了生成元性质并得到最小生成集与秩；推导了码为MHDR和MDS的充要条件，并确定了MHDR码对应的n₀精确值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限链环上的常循环码在代数编码理论中具有重要地位，但此前对任意长度λ-常循环码的生成元构造缺乏系统性的显式方法，且关于其秩、MHDR和MDS性质的表征不够完善。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 利用有限链环R上模λ-常循环的剩余类环R[x]/⟨x^ℓ-λ⟩中某些最小度数多项式，显式构造生成元集合，并证明该集合达到最小生成元数；通过分析生成元性质得到最小生成集与秩；利用剩余域F_q上的挠码刻画MHDR和MDS的充要条件。

Result: (1) 给出了有限链环上任意长度λ-常循环码的显式生成元构造，且生成元个数达到最小；(2) 证明了生成元的若干性质，据此获得了码的最小生成集；(3) 证明码的秩为ℓ-n₀，其中n₀为码中最小度数多项式的次数；(4) 给出了码为MHDR和MDS的充要条件，并确定了MHDR码对应的n₀精确值。

Conclusion: 本文完成了有限链环上λ-常循环码生成元的最小化构造，完整刻画了其代数结构（秩、最小生成集），并为MHDR码和MDS码的判定提供了基于挠码的简洁充要条件，推广和深化了有限链环上常循环码理论。

Abstract: In the present paper, we provide an explicit construction for generators of a $λ$-constacyclic code $\mathcal{C}$ of arbitrary length $\ell$ over a finite chain ring(FCR) $\mathcal{R}$ in terms of certain minimum degree polynomials of the ring $\mathcal{R}[x]/ \langle x^{\ell}-λ\rangle$. Moreover, the proposed construction achieves the minimum possible number of generators. We prove certain properties of this set of generators, using which we obtain a minimal spanning set of $\mathcal{C}$. We also obtain that the rank of $\mathcal{C}$ is $\ell-n_0$, where $n_0$ is the degree of the minimal degree polynomial in $\mathcal{C}$. Finally, we derive necessary and sufficient conditions under which an arbitrary length $λ$-constacyclic code $\mathcal{C}$ over $\mathcal{R}$ is Maximum Hamming Distance with respect to Rank(MHDR) as well as Maximum Distance Separable(MDS) in terms of a torsion code of $\mathcal{C}$ over the residue field $\mathbb{F}_q$ of $\mathcal{R}$. We further determine the exact values for $n_0$ for which $\mathcal{C}$ over $\mathcal{R}$ is MHDR.

### [271] [Generalized Extended Codes with Applications in Entanglement-Assisted Qubit and Qutrit Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02170)
*Yang Li,Martianus Frederic Ezerman,Shitao Li,San Ling,Zhonghua Sun*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文证明了广义扩展码与Hermitian对偶码的单式等价性，并刻画了其Hermitian壳与对偶距离，进而通过Hermitian构造法得到了267个新的EA量子比特码和14个新的EA量子三元码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究广义扩展码的Hermitian结构性质，以系统性地构造性能更优的纠缠辅助量子纠错码（EAQECCs）。

Method: 1. 证明广义扩展码与Hermitian对偶码的单式等价性；2. 将Hermitian壳维数表征为u相对于C+C^{⊥_H}的位置；3. 将Hermitian对偶距离表征为u与C^{⊥_H}最小重量码字的交互；4. 推导同时增大壳维数和对偶距离的条件；5. 应用于Hermitian构造法生成EAQECCs。

Result: 得到了267个新的EA量子比特码（n≤40）和14个新的EA量子三元码（n≤25），其中确认改进了236个量子比特码和8个量子三元码的参数。

Conclusion: 建立了广义扩展码Hermitian壳维数和对偶距离的独立控制判据，为构造更优EAQECCs提供了系统化方法，并获得了大量优于已知结果的新码参数。

Abstract: We prove that any generalized extended code is monomially equivalent to the Hermitian dual of a code which is closely related to a second kind of extended code of $\C^{\perp_{\rm H}}$. Every $[n+1,k+1]_{q^2}$ linear code $\D$ with $d(\D^{\perp_{\rm H}})>1$ is monomially equivalent to the generalized extended code $\C({\bf u},a)$ of an $[n,k]_{q^2}$ linear code $\C$ for a fixed $a\in\F_{q^2}^{*}$ and some ${\bf u}\in\F_{q^2}^{n}$. We then characterize the Hermitian hull and Hermitian dual distance of $\C({\bf u},a)$ in terms of the position of ${\bf u}$ relative to $\C+\C^{\perp_{\rm H}}$ and the interaction between ${\bf u}$ and the minimum weight codewords of $\C^{\perp_{\rm H}}$, respectively. We obtain explicit criteria to independently control the expected Hermitian hull dimension and Hermitian dual distance of $\C({\bf u},a)$. In particular, several conditions for simultaneously increasing the Hermitian hull dimension and the Hermitian dual distance of $\C({\bf u},a)$ are derived. Applying these results to the Hermitian construction for EAQECCs gives us $267$ new EA qubit codes of lengths $n \leq 40$ and $14$ new EA qutrit codes of lengths $n \leq 25$ compared to the best-known codes in Grassl's code tables and the imporvements recorded in very recent works in the literature. Among the new parameter sets, we confirm improvements for $236$ qubit and $8$ qutrit codes.

</details>


### [272] [The Weight Distribution of the Third-Order Reed-Muller Code of Length 2048](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02365)
*Kirill Khoruzhii,Patrick Gelß,Sebastian Pokutta*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文计算了长为2048的三阶Reed-Muller码RM(3,11)的完整权重分布，通过评估所有3691560个非零GL(10,2)-轨道上f+RM(2,10)的陪集权重枚举器实现，确定了每个三次布尔形式的二阶非线性度，并将RM(2,10)的覆盖半径下界从400提升至408，同时通过启发式搜索将RM(6,10)在RM(7,10)中的相对覆盖半径上界从50改进至32。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算高阶Reed-Muller码的权重分布是一个长期存在的困难问题，特别是RM(3,11)的权重分布此前未知。同时，确定布尔函数的非线性度和覆盖半径对编码理论和密码学具有重要意义。

Method: 利用结构定理（非退化三次布尔形式允许非退化超平面限制，除每个奇数维中的单个轨道外），通过计算所有3691560个非零GL(10,2)-轨道的陪集权重枚举器来组装权重分布；并采用启发式搜索改进覆盖半径上界。

Result: 完成了RM(3,11)的权重分布计算；确定了每个三次形式的二阶非线性度，RM(2,10)在RM(3,10)中的相对覆盖半径为408（由179个轨道达到），将覆盖半径下界从400提升至408；RM(6,10)在RM(7,10)中的相对覆盖半径上界改进至32。

Conclusion: 本文成功计算了RM(3,11)的权重分布，显著改进了Reed-Muller码覆盖半径的已知界限，展示了结构定理在解决高维布尔函数编码理论问题中的有效性。

Abstract: We compute the weight distribution of the third-order Reed--Muller code RM(3,11) of length 2048. The weight enumerator is assembled from the coset weight enumerators of f+RM(2,10), evaluated for representatives of all 3691560 nonzero GL(10,2)-orbits of Boolean cubic forms in ten variables. The computation rests on a structural theorem: a nondegenerate Boolean cubic form admits a nondegenerate hyperplane restriction, except for a single orbit in each odd dimension. The same pass determines the second-order nonlinearity of every cubic form: the relative covering radius of RM(2,10) in RM(3,10) is 408, attained on 179 orbits. This raises the best known lower bound on the covering radius of RM(2,10) from 400 to 408. A complementary heuristic search shows that the relative covering radius of RM(6,10) in RM(7,10) is at most 32, improving the previous bound of 50.

### [273] [Generalized Rank Weight and Extended Generalized Poset Weight Defined For Codes Over Rings: A Galois Connection Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02377)
*Yang Xu,Haibin Kan,Guangyue Han*

Main category: cs.IT

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用伽罗瓦连接（Galois connection）作为核心数学框架，将编码理论中的安全缺口、Singleton界、MDS/MRD/Near MRD/i-MRD/准MRD码的特征、逃避子空间性质等问题重新表述为伽罗瓦连接的形式。对于主理想环（特别是链环）上的模，定义并研究GRWs和秩刻画，推导Singleton界和Wei型对偶定理。对于具有合成列的模，定义EGPWs和扩展偏序集刻画，并在任意拟Frobenius环上建立统一的Wei型对偶定理。

Conclusion: 伽罗瓦连接为环上码的广义权重理论提供了一个统一且强大的框架，不仅能够重新表述和统一现有的多个重要结论，还能将结果推广到更广泛的代数结构（如链环、拟Frobenius环），为编码理论的进一步代数化研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: In this paper, we study generalized rank weights (GRWs) and extended generalized poset weight (EGPWs) of codes over rings via a Galois connection approach. First, we show that various coding-theoretic properties related to generalized weights, including security drops of a code employed in wire-tap channel of type II, connections between generalized weights of a Gabidulin code and its associated Delsarte code, (generalized) Singleton bound, MDS discrepancy of a code, characterizations of MDS, near MDS, $i$-MDS, MRD, near MRD, $i$-MRD, (dually) quasi-MRD codes as well as evasive property of subspaces, can be reformulated in terms of Galois connections. Next, we study GRWs and rank profiles defined for modules over principal ideal rings, especially those over chain rings. Generalizing GRWs defined for vector spaces over fields, we establish a singleton bound and a Wei-type duality theorem, characterize MRD, near MRD and dually quasi-MRD codes and determine their GRWs; moreover, we characterize $i$-MRD codes and establish a scattered bound for $(h,h)$-evasive codes over chain rings, generalizing counterpart result established for vector space over finite fields. Finally, we propose and study EGPWs and extended poset profiles defined for modules with a composition series, which in fact form a Galois connection. Generalizing EGPWs defined for modules over finite Galois rings, we establish a Wei-type duality theorem for modules over arbitrary quasi-Frobenius rings, which unifies the two Wei-type duality theorems derived in both \cite{32} and \cite{33}.

### [274] [Ultra-Low-Cost Hybrid Beamforming: A New Static-Connection Architecture with Sparse Phase-Shifter Sharing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02393)
*Honghao Wang,Qingqing Wu,Yifei Wu,Yuxuan Chen,Wen Chen,Derrick Wing Kwan Ng*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种静态连接稀疏移相器架构，通过优化移相器与天线的固定连接矩阵，在子连接混合波束赋形中实现移相器共享，显著降低硬件开销。单射频链场景转化为天线分组问题，多射频链场景采用QoS-MM算法处理混合离散-连续优化。实验表明，在单/多RF链系统中分别减少37.5%和62.5%的移相器数量，同时避免深度零陷和栅瓣退化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统子连接混合波束赋形架构中每个天线仍需专用移相器，导致布局面积、布线、校准和控制开销巨大。为降低硬件成本与复杂度，亟需一种能在保持波束赋形性能的同时大幅减少移相器数量的新型架构。

Method: 提出静态连接稀疏移相器架构：子阵列内天线通过优化后的固定连接矩阵共享一个移相器。单RF链场景将稀疏移相器连接设计转化为天线分组问题，给出结构性质与高效算法；多RF链场景提出QoS-MM算法处理混合离散-连续优化。

Result: 单RF链系统移相器数量减少37.5%，多RF链系统减少62.5%；避免深度零陷和栅瓣退化；保持传统全移相器子连接架构的大部分波束赋形能力。

Conclusion: 硬件高效的混合波束赋形不仅在于减少移相器数量，更关键在于通过优化移相器连接拓扑保留必要的模拟域自由度。

Abstract: Hybrid beamforming is a promising solution for high-frequency multi-antenna wireless systems, but its implementation is constrained by the cost and complexity of analog phase-shifter (PS) networks. Although sub-connected architectures simplify the analog network, their conventional realization still requires a dedicated PS for each antenna, causing considerable layout area, wiring, calibration, and control overheads. To address this issue, this paper proposes a novel static-connection architecture with sparse PSs for ultra-low-cost sub-connected hybrid beamforming, where antennas within each sub-array share a PS through an optimized fixed PS-to-antenna connection matrix. The proposed architecture preserves static connections while enabling dynamic beam control via adaptive PS phase-shift adjustments and digital precoding. For the single-radio-frequency (RF)-chain scenario, the sparse-PS connection design is transformed into an antenna-grouping problem, with analytically characterized structural properties and an efficient algorithm. For the multi-RF-chain scenario, we develop a quality-of-service (QoS)-majorization-minimization (MM) algorithm to handle the mixed discrete-continuous optimization problem. Numerical results demonstrate that the proposed architecture reduces the PS count while preserving most beamforming capability of the traditional full-PS sub-connected architecture. In particular, the proposed design achieves PS-count reductions of 37.5% and 62.5% in single-RF-chain and multi-RF-chain systems, respectively, while avoiding deep-null and grating-lobe degradations associated with deterministic connection schemes. These results provide engineering insights into static sparse-PS sharing: the key to hardware-efficient hybrid beamforming is not merely reducing the PS count, but also preserving essential analog-domain degrees of freedom through optimized PS connection topologies.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两阶段分布式机制：第一阶段各群组基于局部报告选择一对候选位置作为代表；第二阶段从所有代表中输出最终两个设施位置。聚焦于确定性策略证明分布式机制类，分析四种社会目标下的失真度。

Abstract: This paper investigates a constrained distributed heterogeneous two-facility location problem under the max-variant cost model. In this setting, a set of agents with private locations on the real line is partitioned into disjoint groups. The constraint stipulates that facilities must be situated within a given multiset of candidate locations, with the restriction that each candidate location can host at most one facility. Under the max-variant model, an agent's individual cost is defined as the distance from their location to the farthest facility. Our objective is to design strategyproof distributed mechanisms that incentivize agents to report their locations truthfully while approximating social objectives. Such mechanisms operate in two stages: first, for each group, a pair of candidate locations is selected as representatives based solely on local reports; subsequently, the mechanism outputs two final facility locations from the set of all representatives. We focus on a class of deterministic strategyproof distributed mechanisms and establish constant lower and upper bounds on the distortion under four social objectives: Average-of-Average, Max-of-Max, Average-of-Max, and Max-of-Average costs.

### [276] [Facility Location Game with Envy Ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02330)
*Yuan Ding,Wenjing Liu,Xin Chen,Qizhi Fang,Qingqin Nong*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究实数线上单设施选址博弈问题，提出一种新目标函数"嫉妒比"（从公平分配中借鉴的 egalitarian 指标），定义为任意两 agent 效用比值的最大值。在两种自然场景下（设施与 agent 均限定在固定区间内；agent 可在任意点但设施限定在相对区间内），分别给出了最优解、最优确定性策略证明机制（同时也满足群体策略证明性），并为随机机制提供了下界和上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先定义嫉妒比目标函数，然后考虑两种约束场景：1）设施和所有 agent 位置均限制在固定区间内；2）agent 位置可为实数线上任意点，但设施限制在相对区间内。分别求解最优解，设计确定性策略证明（及群体策略证明）机制，并分析随机机制的下界与上界。

Result: 在两种场景下均得到了最优解和最优的确定性策略证明（且群体策略证明）机制。场景1中给出了随机策略证明机制的下界；场景2中给出了一个下界和两个随机策略证明机制的上界。

Conclusion: 将公平分配中的嫉妒比引入设施选址博弈是可行的，且在两种自然场景下都能设计出最优的确定性策略证明机制；随机机制方面仍有进一步优化的空间。

Abstract: We study the one-facility location game on a real line with a new objective called envy ratio. The envy ratio, which is adopted from fair division and represents the egalitarianism, is defined as the maximum over the ratios between any two agents' utilities. We are interested in strategyproof or group strategyproof mechanisms that can minimize the envy ratio objective.
  We consider the model in two settings that can capture natural scenarios: the facility location and all the agents' locations are restricted on a fixed interval; every agent's location can be any point on the real line but the facility location is restricted on a relative interval. In both settings, we obtain the optimal solution and the best deterministic strategyproof mechanism which is also group strategyproof. In the first setting, we provide a lower bound for randomized strategyproof mechanisms. In the second setting, we give a lower bound and two upper bounds for randomized strategyproof mechanisms.

### [277] [Benchmarking Federated Learning and Knowledge Distillation for Point Cloud Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01272)
*Aizierjiang Aiersilan*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个联合评估联邦学习（FL）和知识蒸馏（KD）在3D点云分类中的多种子基准测试，涵盖13种FL算法×10种KD目标的130种组合。主要发现：极端非独立同分布下FL性能急剧下降；KD成功将教师模型压缩74.51%且速度翻倍；但FL+KD组合存在评估陷阱——使用硬标签交叉熵时，即使教师模型崩溃（8.50%），学生仍可达92.94%，建议使用无标签蒸馏避免虚假性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在隐私敏感、资源受限的3D点云分析场景中，数据无法集中且模型需在边缘硬件上运行，现有研究缺乏对联邦学习与知识蒸馏联合效果的系统评估。

Method: 构建包含13种FL算法和10种KD目标的交叉基准（130个组合），在ModelNet40和临床颅缝早闭数据集上进行504次训练，通过多种子评估分析性能。

Result: 1）极端非独立同分布标签偏移下，最强FL方法在ModelNet40上仅达76.32%（集中式92.26%），临床数据75.83%（集中式100%）；2）KD将教师模型压缩74.51%、推理加速约2倍且性能匹配或超越教师；3）硬标签蒸馏存在评估陷阱：教师仅8.50%时学生可达92.94%，产生84.4个百分点的虚假差距。

Conclusion: 建议评估FL-KD流水线时使用无标签蒸馏方法，以确保报告的性能真实反映联邦教师模型的质量而非代理标签。

Abstract: Deploying 3D point cloud analysis in privacy-sensitive, resource-constrained settings faces two barriers: data cannot be centralized, and models must run on limited edge hardware. We present a multi-seed benchmark jointly evaluating federated learning (FL) and knowledge distillation (KD) for 3D point cloud classification. It spans 13 FL algorithms and 10 KD objectives (a 130-pair cross-product) across 504 training runs, evaluated on ModelNet40 and a clinical craniosynostosis dataset. We report three findings. First, under extreme non-IID label skew, standalone FL degrades sharply: on ModelNet40, the strongest method reaches 76.32% against a 92.26% centralized reference; on clinical data, the best reaches 75.83% against 100%. Second, distillation successfully compresses the teacher into a student 74.51% smaller and roughly twice as fast at inference, often matching or surpassing the teacher. Third, the combined pipeline exposes an evaluation pitfall: when distillation keeps a hard-label cross-entropy term on a labeled proxy split, a collapsed federated teacher (8.50%) paired with Logit-MSE still yields a 92.94% student. This 84.4-point gap reflects the proxy labels rather than the federated model, reusing the very labels whose privacy motivated federation. Objectives without hard labels instead track teacher quality ($r \approx 0.99$) and collapse when the teacher does. We therefore recommend evaluating FL-KD pipelines with label-free distillation so reported accuracy reflects the federated teacher, not the proxy.

### [278] [FUSE: A Partitioned Field-Exchange Framework for Coupling Physics Simulations in FEBio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01428)
*Steve A. Maas,Farhan Muhib,Jeffrey A. Weiss*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: FUSE是一个基于FEBio的分区耦合插件框架，通过结构化场交换实现独立定义的物理模型之间的通信，采用时间解耦策略处理快慢不同时间尺度的多物理场耦合问题，在软骨损伤和骨愈合等生物力学应用中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算生物力学需要结合力学、传输、化学和生物调控的多尺度模型，但现有方法依赖自定义脚本或外部软件管线，限制了模型复用和开发效率。

Method: 提出FUSE框架，采用分区耦合方法，通过结构化场交换使主模型（长时间尺度）与次模型（短时间尺度）通信，利用FEBio现有数据映射、输出字段和用户指定过滤器实现场交换，无需修改底层求解器。

Result: FUSE能够复现参考耦合解，支持双向传输、空间场映射和过滤交换；在软骨损伤（力学加载与化学降解耦合）和骨愈合（组织形成与力学反馈耦合）两个示例应用中成功验证。

Conclusion: 通过将耦合逻辑与物理实现分离，FUSE为在FEBio中构建可维护的多物理场工作流提供了实用机制。

Abstract: Computational biomechanics increasingly requires models that combine mechanics, transport, chemistry, and biological regulation across different spatial and temporal scales. The FEBio simulation software provides extensive open-source capabilities for modeling these processes using monolithic approaches. However, assembling independently developed physics models into reproducible coupled workflows remains challenging. Existing approaches often require custom scripts or external software pipelines, which can limit model reuse and complicate development. We present FUSE, the FEBio Unified Simulation and Exchange framework, a partitioned coupling plugin that enables separately defined FEBio models to communicate through structured field exchange. FUSE is designed for problems that are best solved independently, particularly when fast mechanical responses influence slower biological or chemical evolution. The framework uses a time-decoupled strategy in which a primary model advances on the longer time scale, while one or more secondary models are repeatedly initialized, supplied with updated fields, solved over shorter time horizons, with results returned to the primary model. Field exchange utilizes existing FEBio data maps, output fields, and user-specified filters, allowing coupled workflows to be constructed without modifying the underlying solvers. The framework was able to reproduce reference coupled solutions while handling bidirectional transfer, spatial field mapping, and filtered exchange of model variables. Example applications demonstrated coupling between mechanical loading and chemical degradation in injured cartilage and interaction between biological tissue formation and mechanical feedback during bone healing. By separating coupling logic from physics implementation, FUSE provides a practical mechanism for building maintainable multiphysics workflows within FEBio.

</details>


### [279] [TO-Master: an LLM-agent framework for automated topology optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01812)
*Haoju Lin,Wenchang Zhang,Weipeng Xu,Xiang Li,Tian Xu,Tianju Xue*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出TO-Master，一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体框架，将有限元拓扑优化转化为对话式、工具编排的工作流程，用户通过自然语言即可完成从几何准备、网格生成到优化求解的全过程，无需编写代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑优化虽已成熟，但其使用仍需大量人工操作（几何准备、网格生成、边界条件分配、求解器设置、后处理），这一实现壁垒限制了其在专家工作流之外的应用。

Method: 构建LLM智能体框架TO-Master：从自然语言指令（可选的网格、几何或图像输入）出发，智能体选择计算工具、构建有限元拓扑优化模型、检查网格和边界条件、启动基于灵敏度的优化（含类型化求解器参数）。支持生成/上传网格、图像转网格、2D/3D结构柔度最小化、热传导、多载荷工况、应力约束优化及工程几何结构。

Result: 数值实验表明：TO-Master能够复现标准基准结果，解决更复杂的工程实例，返回优化结果、场分布、收敛历史及交互式工件，无需用户编写代码。消融研究表明：工具使用规则、内部推理指导和少样本示例对模糊用户输入下的鲁棒公式构建至关重要。

Conclusion: 通过结合LLM智能体编排与确定性有限元和优化工具，TO-Master消除了繁琐设置和常规模型构建的负担，降低了拓扑优化的建模门槛，同时保持了可靠的数值工作流。

Abstract: Topology optimization (TO) has become a mature computational design method, but using it still requires substantial manual effort in geometry preparation, mesh generation, boundary-condition assignment, solver setup, and postprocessing. This implementation barrier limits the use of TO outside expert workflows, even when differentiable finite element solvers are available. This work introduces TO-Master, a large language model (LLM) agent framework that turns finite-element-based TO into a conversational, tool-orchestrated workflow. From natural language instructions and optional mesh, geometry, or image inputs, the agent selects computational tools, constructs finite element TO models, checks meshes and boundary conditions, and launches sensitivity-based optimization with typed solver arguments. The framework supports generated and uploaded meshes, image-to-mesh conversion, 2D and 3D structural compliance minimization, thermal conduction, multiple load cases, stress-constrained optimization, and engineering geometries. Numerical experiments show that TO-Master can reproduce standard benchmark results and solve more complex engineering examples while returning optimized results, field distributions, convergence histories, and interactive artifacts without user-written code. An instruction ablation study further shows that tool-usage rules, internal reasoning guidance, and few-shot examples are critical for robust formulation under ambiguous user input. By combining LLM-agent orchestration with deterministic finite element and optimization tools, TO-Master removes the burden of trivial setup and routine model construction, lowers the modeling barrier of TO, and preserves a reliable numerical workflow. The TO-Master platform is available online at https://www.bohrium.com/en/apps/to-master.

</details>


### [280] [Predicting Heterogeneous Treatment Effects Of Building Energy Saving Retrofits Using Causal Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01891)
*Kevin Zalipski,David Zapata Gonzalez,Oliver Müller*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了多种因果机器学习估计器（元学习器、DoubleML）在建筑改造中的节能效果估计性能，发现DoubleML在存在选择偏差时估计误差最小，为大规模能效政策评估提供了方法论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 信息系统研究日益依赖机器学习预测复杂社会技术系统的结果，但预测模型无法识别因果效应。在建筑改造领域，对节能效果的无偏估计对气候政策和投资决策至关重要，而改造采纳行为受家庭和建筑特征影响，这些特征同时影响能耗，导致预测性ML产生有偏估计。

Method: 构建了一个物理基础仿真环境，其中真实处理效应和现实采纳偏差已知；系统比较了包括S-Learner、T-Learner、X-Learner在内的元学习器和DoubleML等多种因果ML估计器，涵盖多种改造干预类型。

Result: DoubleML实现了最低的估计误差，尤其是在复杂的围护结构改造场景中表现突出。正交化处理分配方法显著改善了因果效应估计。

Conclusion: 正交化处理分配能够改善因果效应估计，为大规模建筑节能改造和政策评估提供了方法基础。

Abstract: Information Systems research increasingly relies on machine learning (ML) to predict outcomes in complex sociotechnical systems, yet predictive models are not designed to identify causal effects. This limitation is particularly critical in building retrofits, where unbiased estimates of energy savings are essential for climate policy and investment decisions. Because retrofit adoption is shaped by household and building characteristics that also affect energy consumption, predictive ML can yield biased effect estimates. This paper systematically benchmarks leading causal ML estimators, including metalearners (S-, T- and X-Learners) and DoubleML across multiple retrofit interventions. To enable this comparison, we construct a physically grounded simulation in which true treatment effects and realistic adoption biases are known. Results show that DoubleML achieves the lowest estimation errors, particularly for complex envelope retrofits. These findings demonstrate that orthogonalising the treatment assignment improves causal effect estimation and provides a methodological foundation for large-scale energy retrofit and policy evaluation.

</details>
